Translated Text (Page 4):
8 7 Introduction It was a few years ago that I had an idea in my heart to compile a brief but comprehensive and authentic book about Sadat Barah, in which the current details of the historical figures of Sadat Barah are established and in which the famous people of the nation The accomplishments of the people and their war exploits should be well brought out so that after studying them, people can be enlightened about the characteristics of this tribe and their services and their importance in history and the achievements of this tribe and its achievements from a historical perspective. The golden achievements are presented only nominally. However, a lot of real work has been done on Sadat Azam in Pakistan. In this regard, Dr. Safdar Sen Sahib has rendered commendable services there. Sadat Baraha is full of bravery and his services before the Mughal Sultans are of great importance and his loyalty to the Mughal emperors is truly admirable. Sadat Barah played a very important role in the establishment of the Mughal empires in India and in keeping them organized, the living proof of this is the victories of the Mughal sultans, which depended on the immense courage of Sadat Barah&#39;s nobles and their great fighting skills. Stayed on. These were the salient features of this tribe, thanks to which the Mughal emperors were able to identify complex and complex Mahats and their exact location. Compiling such a book as it was successful in the head, but it was not an easy matter for a sad reason, but in any case, due to the great encouragement of loved ones and friends, I decided to do this work. A long time ago, the late Syed Muzaffar Ali Khan Manna, the great grandfather of Rakim al-Haruf, had also compiled a history of Sadat under the name of &quot;Tarikh Sadat Bahira&quot; but for some reason it could not be published, which is really a pity. Sadat Baraha in India. But very few writers have paid attention to the fact that the writers of history acted short-sightedly and ignored the valuable services of this tribe So, in such a way that they only looked at Sadat Barah&#39;s flaws and completely ignored all his two good qualities, they called Sadat Azam a liar and a traitor and heaped hatred and hatred on him, which is undoubtedly from the truth. There is a veil and behind this hatred, the spirit of jealousy and jealousy seems to be working

Translated Text (Page 5):
10 4 Sadat Bar is carrying out this research work which is an encouraging step in this regard and which will result in a useful and very effective explanation of the characteristics and achievements of this tribe and their achievements. We sincerely hope from such researchers that they will be able to shed light on the right side of history without acting on feelings about Sadat Azam and present the importance of his existence and his services in history in a very fair manner. will be able to do so that the history can be properly reflected in the book under review, &quot;Sadat Barah&#39;s historical review, I think it is important to submit only that this is not a detailed history related to Sadat Barah, but a review in summary, in which Sadat-e-Azam A glimpse of his services and sacrifices can be seen. While compiling this book, all my efforts have been so that no unnecessary and absurd events can be included in it, but still a few incidents have come to our mind. I have been hearing from my elders. Such incidents which I have written are almost based on reality and they cannot be considered traditional. In addition, I have written controversial topics and incidents What has been avoided so that there is no possibility of any unnecessary discussion. All the necessary references and references are present in the book so that there is no room for any kind of doubt. In Asiatic Society. I am extremely grateful to Calcutta for giving me permission to quote and translate from Dr. Beni Parshad&#39;s book &quot;Maasir al-Amrar&quot; (English translation). Apart from this, I am also very grateful to Syed Zaheer Abbas resident of town Jansath and Syed Hamid Hussain resident of Mauza Sri Rasoolpur that they have helped me a lot from time to time in compiling this book. Finally, the readers are requested to inform Khaksar with their valuable opinions. Only Akhr: Syed Sulaiman Ali Khan b. Oh Ring Mahal - Janth. P. And Muzaffar district. U.P

The Magnificient Moghuls
by: Tikam Rammani.
Translated Text (Page 6):
12 11 I Sadat Bara Sadat Barja is the name of a well-known and influential tribe of Sayyids in India, most of whose families are settled in the Doaba region, now located in Muzaffarnagar district. The special places of Sadat Barah are Bajanasat Samheera Majheera - Jawara Kho Jara - Hebatpur Pledi - Miranpur - Ha Kampur Ki Tehora. Tons or fleet. But Wali Bara. Morna - Case of Muzaffar Nagar Khas. Bihari Sindha Delhi - Chittor - Kowal. Bilaspur Bhutora. Sarai Rasoolpur Yora. Julie etc. Apart from this, few families of Sadat Baraha are settled in Bijnor and Mir Khas district located in Nagina. Scholars and historians give different interpretations and meanings of the word &quot;twelve&quot;. For example, the word twelve in &quot;To Zak&quot; and &quot;Taqabah&quot; is given to correspond to the number twelve (12). Twelve is a Hindi word, i.e. Leh Ain Akbari (English translation) Author: H. Calcutta edition in Balakh according to &quot;Tuzak Choun&quot; The population of Sadat in the Doaba area consisted of twelve villages, so this tribe was called Sadat Barah, which later became known as Sadat Barah due to frequent usage. Dr. Bar Nair has recorded the situation and events of that time in the book &quot;Waqa&#39;i Seir Wa Turism&quot; and wherever Sadat is mentioned in the footnotes, he has used the word &quot;Barahwal&quot; along with his name. &quot;Barahwal&quot; means &quot;twelve people&quot;. Some scholars also believe that because the heir of Sadat, the great Sayyid Abdullah al-Hasan, known as Abul Farah, came from outside India, that is, the country of Iraq, therefore, his generation is called Sadat Bahrah. It was called by the name of which later changed to Sadat Baraha due to frequent use. In his English book &quot;The Magnificent Mughal&quot;, Mr. Sekim Ramzani also expresses similar views and writes: Shadat Barah was always appointed in the front corner of the Mughal army and this right became his legacy. &quot; Another hypothesis regarding the word Baraha which is quite strong in its place is that all the Sadats are Baraha because of their religious belief, they are Ashri Shia, i.e. they are followers of twelve Imams, so these people are The Magnificent Moghuls by: Tikam Rammani.

Translated Text (Page 7):
14 13 It was called &quot;Sadat Bara&quot;, which later became famous as Sadat Bar due to frequent use. However, whether the use of the word &quot;twelve&quot; is appropriate or not can be a long discussion, so regardless of this discussion, we will use the word &quot;twelve&quot; in our book with Sadat, because we think According to Sadat, the use of the word twelve is appropriate. Apart from this, the word &quot;twelve&quot; seems to be used with Sadat in all the historical books that we have come across. Therefore, we will also use the word twelve. The family of Sadat Baraha is famous for its courage and bravery. Courage is in the blood of the people of this tribe and this is their distinguishing feature. His brave deeds are still preserved in history. Along with bravery, courage and immense enthusiasm, simplicity and austerity are also included in their attributes. The members of this tribe fearlessly participated in most of the wars of the Mughal era and fought the difficult battles in front of the Mughal Sultans with their immense bravery and shedding their precious blood. In all Mughal history, there is no such battle in which the men of Sadat Baraha did not show their best fighting performance and did not risk their lives to save the Timurid sultans. Emperor Akbar and all the Mughal Sultans after him took full advantage of Sadat&#39;s bravery and his fighting skills, and Sadat Bareh spared no effort in paying their dues. The magnificent buildings built by the famous nobles of Sadat Barah in their respective places and areas are still a manifestation of their glory and majesty. Although most of the buildings are now in a dilapidated state, looking at them even today, you can feel the importance of Sadat and the influence of this tribe, for example, the four big gates in the town of Jansath, which are also quite high and of which Kar Hati can be easily passed and there is a very beautiful mosque, apart from this the town itself has a Diwan Khana, a large mansion and a bath. In the town of Miranpur Rizla Muzaffarnagar, the magnificent buildings of Ko Tala and Garhti Ghira still exist in a dilapidated condition. Sadat&#39;s memorial, a raised gate and garhi buildings still exist at Mauza Kehlawara. In the same way, a high gate and the building of Imam Barade can be seen in the Mauza Samkhal Heera. Some people have doubts about Sadat&#39;s bravery, to comfort them and to satisfy their unbridled arrogance, we quote here a quote from &quot;Ain Akbari&quot; by H. Balakh (published in Calcutta) which studies Evidence of Sadat&#39;s bravery is provided. By showing the essence of his bravery, Sadat Barah defeated the Khanazads of Mewat, the Sadats of Amruha and the royal Safavid family.

Destroyed 16 15 from the beginning and became an immense force and excelled them all. His struggle in the battlefield was unparalleled. It was against his ego to step back from the field once he had given in the battle. Due to simplicity, sometimes they used to attack the enemy without thinking without any fear, which often resulted in success and success kissing their feet. Emperor Jahangir&#39;s words about Sadat Baraha are also worth seeing. Some people have doubts about their true lineage, but their courage and bravery is an undeniable proof of their being a Sayyid. Among all the battles of this empire, there is no battle in which these people have not distinguished themselves and some of their people have not been useful. Mirza used to say to Aziz that: Sadat Bara are the people who turn away the calls that are coming down on this kingdom. The truth is that this is a fact. As further proof of Sadat Baraha&#39;s bravery and serving the Timurid sultans with sacrifice and faithfulness, an incident which is written in the history of Sadat Bahira&quot; Author: Nah Tuzak Jahan Giri Urdu Translation Saleem Wahid Saleem - Printed - Lahore - The late Kasbah Jansath (unpublished) is written here. He was a resident and employed as an army officer in Humayun Badshah&#39;s government He was in his homeland, when he gathered all his dear friends and went to help Humayun He immediately turned to Agra and very soon met Humayun as the Afghans were in pursuit of Humayun. Syed Sahib also remained under the yoke of our good wishes. On some occasions the Afghans came close. You fought and stopped them and very young men had a busy fight and gave great courage. Most of your loved ones and friends came to work in these shows. In the same way, fighting with the Afghans, they arrived at Attock River, which is called Sindh. At that time very few men were left together. Humayun wanted to cross the river when the enemy came in pursuit. Humayun also asked Syed Sahib to follow his path. You have the answer.

22 21 221 After stabilizing the government in the region and after the situation became satisfactory enough, Sultan Mahmud gathered a lot of wealth and left for his homeland Ghazni from Band Tuan, and the Sayyid Sahib also owned the estates of Sarasand and Kalanur. But leaving behind his four sons, Sultan Mahmud returned with him and reached his homeland from Ghazni to Iraq, died in Shifa and was buried there. Here we consider it necessary to remove this misunderstanding of some people who say that Sadat Bar is every Iranian race. The fact is that Sadat is of Arab descent, because the heir of this tribe, Sayyed Abdullah Al-Hassan, known as Abu Farah Wasti&#39;s original homeland, was Iraq. A few other traditions are also narrated in connection with the arrival of Siyar Abdullah al-Hasan known as Abul Farah Wasti in India. For example, there is a tradition that when Halaku Khan invaded Baghdad and conquered it, a large number of people fled from there and went to Ghazni due to fear and terror. Therefore, the people who left the four sons of Syed Abdullah Al-Hassan in Mutarmand and Kalanur after the conquest of Punjab by Sultan Mahmud of Baghdad remained permanently in Punjab and the descendants of these four sons are the total of twelve Sadats. The names of the four sons of Sayyid Mosawuf are: Tahanpuri) Sayyed Ward and Sayyed Dard - 2- Sayyed Abul Fazl (Chhat Nuzi) Sayyed Abul Firas (Kondi Wali Hai) - 4- Sayyed Najmuddin (Jeezi) Sayyed Abdullah Al Hasan known as Abul Farah Wasti (2) (3) Syed Abul Fazl Syed Abul Firas Syed Najmuddin (Jezi) (Tahanpuri) Ucha Terodi) (Kondiwal) lived in Triq, Syed Abdullah Al Hasan was also included in them. Upon reaching Ghazni, the above four sajzadagans settled in the region of Punjab in this way and joined the government of Sultan Mahmud. And later came to India with him. This tradition is present in Ain Akbari. In any case, how Syed Abdullah Al Hasan came to India is a different issue, but it is proven that his original homeland is Iraq and he was of Arab descent. In Balakh. In the Calcutta edition, &quot;Amin Akbari&quot; the name of Syed Abu Al-Fazl is written as Syed Abul Fazil, which is incorrect. Dr. Syed Safdar Hussain has also accepted the name Sayeda Bu Al-Fras as correct in his book &quot;Saidan Badshah Gar&quot;.

Qutb-ul-Mulk Syed Hasan Ali Khan and Amir Al-Amra Rishid Main Ali Khan, who have become famous in history as the &quot;king brothers&quot;, belonged to the Shahnpuri branch of Sadat. Due to the conquest of India by Sultan Shahabuddin Ghori in Malaya, Sultan Mahmud&#39;s empire and government was shaken and his successor Malik Khusrau was arrested in India. Thus settling in Sultan Mahmud, after the sudden killing of Sultan Shahabuddin Ghori, Qutbuddin Aibak took control of Annan Sultanate in his hands. This sultan was a very good-hearted and truly generous person. He wrote it in &quot;History of India English Author: Michael Edward. London Edition 946.&quot;

Translated Text (Page 13):
26 25 Keeping in mind the important services of Sadat Baraha and their loyalty to the royal government, the area between the Ganges River and the Jumna River, which after Sayyed Hasan Fakhruddin, other Sadats also turned to the two Aba area. So Syed Jalal Khan Mir, who is Syed Dawood Ibn Abul Farah, gave two Aba Gangu Jumans to the famous chiefs of Sadat Barah. was in the eighth Pashtu and whose homeland was Punjab located in Nahinpur, thus the Sultan also favored Sadat and strengthened and stabilized his base throne i.e. Delhi. Syed Man Fakhruddin who was in the back of Syed Abul Fazl Ibn Syed Abdullah Al Hasan Abul Farah Wasti, and on his way from his native Punjab to the capital of Delhi at Chhat Banur, he often stopped at Hera (Muzaffarnagar district, which was settled by Raja Sambhal and He was the ruler of this area and Raja Sambhal used to be a guest here for the purpose of sightseeing and hunting and he used to camp here for a long time and entertain himself after the death of Raja Sambhal. As a protection for herself and to save her jagir, the widow decided to pay a special compensation for herself on a few conditions if she martyred her total jagir Syed Hasan Fakhruddin. Apart from that, no other person was suitable in the eyes of the queen. After the entire region was established and after establishing his rule here, Syed Hasan Fakhruddin moved his entire family from Mouza Chhat in Punjab to Mouza Dhansari. Rizla took up residence in Muzaffarnagar. Thus, this family became famous. Sayyid Aiyuz, who was the son of Sayyid Abul Firas Ibn Abul Farah Wasti, was a resident of Mauza Kundli Punjab and settled in Mauza Mujra (Muzaffar Nagar district) after piercing Kundli, so this family became famous as Sadat Kondi Wal. This place is located four miles east of Jansath. Similarly, Sayyid Hussain who was in the back of Sayyid Najamuddin Ibn Abul Farah Wasti came from Mouz Jajiz Punjab and settled in Mouz Puldi (District Muzaffarnagar). This mouz is located four miles south of Jansat. In 12 AD, Sultan Qutbuddin Aibak died suddenly while playing polo and the throne was succeeded by Sultan Shamsuddin Al-Tamish. This is how this family continued to read Mauza Sambha. So Syed Muhammad Sughri was given Jagir in Parganah Hardoi and this area was settled in Sadat for a while. It was accepted because this family came here from Chatta Banur, so this family was called Chatta Banuri.

Among the descendants of 32 and 31, Syed Aiyuz and others came to Mujaira and Muzaffarnagar district from Punjab located in Kondli and settled. There was nothing else in this area except forests and a special type of grass grew here. The people of Kondliwal here were ordinary laborers from the beginning and their livelihood was very difficult. Economically, their conditions were very bad. After some time these people spread to settle in Bashpur-Tasang, Tand Bhera etc. Sadat Ko Nadiwal in Muzaffarnagar district are the following: Mujira Khas, Balipura, Sing, Mandhira, Bhutora, Kho Jera Hashimpur, Maulana Kalan, Chandpur crossing the Ganges Shadat Jamezi or Jagiri of Syed Najamuddin and Syed Qamaruddin. The descendants migrated from Mauza Jamezi or Jagir Punjab and settled in Mauza Badoli near the Yamuna River. After some time Syed Qamaruddin, Syed Hussain and others left Mauza Badoli and migrated to Mauza Pa, which is south of Jansath. Syed Qamaruddin&#39;s Zamindari Mouz Chandvadh. Chand wadi Tulsipur and Khedi and Ghira read meds report Ain Akbari&quot; (English) Author: H. Balakh was in Calcutta. His children lived in these places. Now there is no person of Sadat in Mauza Chandwara Demipur. The important places of Sadat Jachizi are: Pedi, Badoli Chand, etc. The town of Jansath, district Muzaffarnagar, has old historical traditions. The base of the Pandas was Hastanapur, which is located in the valley of the river Ganges, so this area was their clearing and a temple is known as Sada Shia and both of them are built as memorials of the same time. When the Pandus lost their entire kingdom to the Ra&#39;s in gambling, there was a dispute over the place of residence. At first Roane had returned the kingdom, but after this victory he refused to return it. A meeting was held at the same place for settlement. Rajagan, Maharajgan and Sri Krishnaji Maharaj attended this sabha. Before the start of the sabha, Jahadev Ji was worshiped as per the tradition. Where this pooja took place. Translated Text (Page 18):
36 35 In Akbari Constitution, &quot;Mansab&quot; has been interpreted as follows:- Mansab is a civil and military rank which was created and invented by King Akbar. Before Akbar the Great, the kings had only two types of Sardars of Hundred and Thousand, but Akbar issued them as a rule. There are two parts in the position, one is the caste and the other is the rider. Caste indicates the monthly salary of the official and his military collection. During Akbar&#39;s time and till the end of Alamgir&#39;s reign, the first rank chieftains were given a position of five thousand. Sat Hazari, the minister or one or two special companions used to get it. Sayyid Mahmud Khan was appointed to discipline the Twelver Daqtabas by Mashar Al-Amrar (English translation) who had captured Nagor and Ajmer. In the third year of Jalus Akbari, Syed Mahmud Baraha captured the fort of Jataun from the possession of the Rajputs and occupied it himself. After entering the regular service of Akbar Badshah, he was given a jagir in the suburbs of Delhi. Eighteen years later, when the king visited Gujrat in the procession of Akbari, Syed Mahmud along with twelve other royal officers had already left for Gujrat and joined the royal army at Mir Tha. In Akbar Azam&#39;s battle with Muhammad Hussain, Syed Mahmud Baz Harsha was the support of the army and fought with great bravery. At the end of the same year, Syed Mahmood is bar. Sayyid Muhammad Amruha and other Sadats along with the people of Baraha conquered and occupied this area by Raja Madhu. He died about 10 years after that. Sayyid Mahmud Yeh Hai&quot; Sayyid Mahmud Khan was the first person among the Sadats who held every two thousand posts in the Emirate. Actually, Sayyid Mahmud Khan was an employee of Barah Bayram Khan. The procession in the first year of Akbar Azam. In Sayyid Mahmud Bar hai by Akbar Azam to compete with Hemu Bakal, Sayyid Mahmud Bar was Nadli Dal to Har Sadat He takes care of it. In the second year of the procession of Akbar Badshah, Ghulam Syed Qasim and Syed Hashim Ba Rahabhe - English translation - Volume II by Dr. Beni Parshad - Asiatic Society. Calcutta (excerpt from Manj al-Amra English translation)

نے سید قاسم بارہہ اور دوسرے سرداروں کو شہر کی حفاظت کے لیے وہاں

آپ بار بار مظفر کے خلاف اور جام جو کچھ کا زمین دار تھا بہادری کے ساتھ
بڑے ۔ خان گر جو بڑے کچھ کا زمین دار تھا اس کا مقابلہ بھی آپنے بخوبی کیا۔

کی بجائے خان اعظم کو کہ مقرر ہوئے اور اس کی زبردست جنگ سلطان

Translated Text (Page 19):
38 37 Sheed Qasim and Syed Basham Barah were the sons of Syed Mahmud Khan Barah. Syed Qasim Akbar was appointed to compete with Khan Alam in the seventeenth year procession of Muhammad Hussain Mirza who had fled to the Deccan after being defeated by Khan Azim. In the 21st year of Syed Hashim Akbar Badshah&#39;s procession, he was appointed with Raja Rai Singh to crush the rebellion of Sultan Devaru, who was the king of Sard. Syed Hashim gained a lot of fame in this campaign of Sarohi. He accompanied Shahbaz Khan in the Akbari procession in the twenty-second year to discipline the Rana. In the 25th year of the procession of Akbari, Chandrasin son of Maldev raised the flag of rebellion against Akbar Azam, then Sayyid Qasim Rashid Basham Bar, who was a feudal lord in the province of Ajmer, came against Chandrasin along with other Mughal chieftains and fought. A few Rasin left Sayyed Qasim Baraha and other chiefs there to protect the city. After that Syed Qasim was also appointed to protect Patan. You repeatedly fought against Muzaffar and the Jam who was the owner of the land with bravery. Khangar, who was the landlord of a large tract of land, was also well fought by him. In the thirty-seventh year of Jalus Akbari, when Khan Azam was appointed as the head of Gujarat instead of Mirza Khan, and he had a great battle with Sultan Muzaffar Khan, Syed Qasim Bar was present at the forefront. After that, Syed Qasim participated with Sultan Murad in the Deccan campaign and he was stationed at Meera in this war with the Deccans. You created great and great fame with great bravery and died in 109 AD. Syed Hashim held the post of 1500 times each. Syed Hashim Barah settled Mouza Bashampur (Muzaffarnagar district) and fled there. In the same year, Muzaffar Khan Gujarati made a big fuss and he was buried on both of them. Along with Dukhan, there was a battle with Muzaffar Khan. In this battle, Syed Hashim was also killed He was injured in this battle. Later, Mirza Khan A. Al-Amrar is available in English translation - Volume II - Asiatic Society - Calcutta. The tomb of Sayyed Qasim Bara is in a dilapidated condition near Mauza Khedi Quraysh Still Exists. (Author) Syed Ali Asghar Bar Har Maaldaq Be Saif Khan (Quoted by Mather Al-Amrar English Translation) - Volume II Dr. Beni Par Shaad - Asia Tak Society - Calcutta.

Translated Text (Page 20):
40 39 You were the son of Syed Mahmood Khan Baraha. You had a special place in the eyes of King Jahangir from the time when Jahangir was a prince. Wadsid Ali was very kind to Asghar and he was always in front of him. When Khusrau started a disturbance in Jahangir&#39;s kingdom, Jahangir appointed Sheikh Farid Murtaza to discipline him. Syed Ali Asghar was at the forefront of Sheikh Farid&#39;s army. The battle of Ghamsan took place between the two armies near Lahore. Syed Ali Asghar fought bravely. You got seventeen wounds. Jahangir immediately appointed him to the position of 2,000 foot and 2,000 cavalry. After some time he was appointed as Faujdar of Hissar. In the fifth year, you were given darkness and knowledge in Jahangir. Syed Ali Asghar participated in Rana Amarsingh&#39;s campaign along with Jahan Gir Khurram in the eighth year procession. In the 10th year, he was injured in a procession in Jahangir and he was sent to the Deccan along with Prince Parvez and died of cholera. King Jahangir&#39;s confession about Syed Ali Asghar Bara, which he himself penned in &quot;Tuzak Jahangiri&quot; We write here word for word: Ali Asghar Bara is second to none in performing bravery and service and Mahmud Khan Baraha&#39;s son was one of the great nobles in my father&#39;s court and I gave him the title of &quot;Saif Khan&quot;. I have always included him in places where I have had only a few confidants with me, he has never used drugs in his life and has been abstinent from his youth. Insha Allah, he will reach a very high position. I also gave him the position of Saifpur, which is located in Meerut district. (Author) Sayyid Salabat Khan Barah (Quoted by Mashar Al-Amrar) Sayyid&#39;s name was Sayyid Sultan and Khattab Khan was the son of Sayyid Bai Yazid and the grandson of Sayyid Hashim Barah. He was one of the senior military officers of Prince Dara Shikoh and Dara had great confidence in him. For twenty-four years, he was assigned to the province of Punjab as the deputy of Prince Darashkoh in Jalus Shah Jahan Badshah and held the title and position of Salabat Khan with 2,000 foot and 400 cavalry. You were also given an elephant. In the same year, on the recommendation of the said Prince, he was sent as the Deputy Governor of Dar Allahabad. You have managed well. Calcutta

42 41 established peace and order. In the twenty-fifth year of Jalus Shah Jahan Badshah, knowledge was given to him. Apart from this, Naqara was also granted to you. In the thirtieth year of procession Shad Jahan Badshah, Salabat Khan captured Noop Singh who was a landowner near Allahabad and presented him in the court and due to his efforts, Anoop Singh was also attached to the royal services. There were 44 43 children. In the tenth year procession of Shah Jahan Badshah, he held the position of 800 footmen and 600 horsemen. In the 19th year, Syed Shahab along with Prince Murad Bakhsh was appointed in Balkh and Badakhshan campaign in Jalus Shah Jahan. Before his departure, he was given a cloak and a horse by the king. He showed bravery in the fight with the Iranians. In the thirteenth year, his position was increased to fifteen hundred footmen and a few hundred horsemen in the procession. In the twenty-eighth year of Shah Jahan Badshah procession, he along with Jamlat-ul-Mulk Saadullah Khan attacked Junont. In the thirtieth year, along with Moazzam Khan, Syed Shahab was sent to the Deccan in the service of Aurangzeb, where he performed many outstanding deeds. In the thirty-first year, his rank was increased to 2,500 infantry and 12,000 cavalry in the procession of Shah Jahan Badshah and he was given the title of &quot;Sher Khan&quot;. Later he was appointed Faujdar in the fort of Benasur (Andor). In the battle of Samogarh he was with Dara Shikoh but after his defeat he joined the service of Aurangzeb. In the battle with Sultan Shuja Syed Shabab Zulfiqar Khan Muhammad The tomb of Sayyid Shahab Bara, who was in command of the artillery by Beg, which is four miles north of the town of Jansath, is still in good condition (Molfat). The crown prince remained with Prince Khurram, but later he was sent to the presence of King Jahangir He was very angry. After he became king, Khurram did not show mercy to him, because of which he returned to his homeland. This campaign was taking a long time due to the pride and stubbornness of the commander-in-chief, Mahabat Khan, and all the big chiefs, such as Hasan Duran Bahadur, were very worried. 46 45 Mahabat Khan would give a clear answer and said that you should give a certain date that the fort will be conquered by that date. Otherwise, we would not accept your leadership, but Mahabat Khan still insisted that the siege of the fort should be continued. Syed Jafar Shujaat Khan was against continuing the siege of the fort as the rainy season was approaching. Finally Prince Shuja ordered to break the siege and withdraw the troops. Mahabat Khan was forced to agree to this because of much trouble. In the 10th year of Jalus Shah Jahan Badshah, Syed Jafar Baraha was appointed governor of Allahabad. At that time there was a lot of chaos in Allahabad. Therefore, Syed Jafar was given more troops than his position so that he could properly manage. You worked very hard in explaining the complex issues of Allahabad province and in reprimanding the prisoners. While he was staying in Guna Erji, he fell ill due to heavy drinking and died here in 11th year. Syed Jafar Shujaat Khan was always a very high-ranking official and looked like a prince. Shah Jahan Badshah thought of you a lot. You were a frank and very frank person. Your Sayyadabul Muzaffar Khan always used to look at you. His son Syed Muzaffar Shah Jahan held the position of 12 hundred footmen and 800 horsemen in the ninth year of the procession. He was given the title of &quot;Himat Khan&quot;. His second son Syed Najabat Khan held the position of 1,000 foot and 500 horsemen. Syed Jafar belonged to the Sadat branch of Kundliwal. Ganga is located in Bijnoor district. He was the brother of Syed Hajo Barah Sadat. He was a very brave and courageous person Bhijo Barah died in Najhera (district of Muzaffarnagar). 48 47 Syed Qasim Khan Bar Ho married Noor Jahan Begum&#39;s sister Meena Begum and in this way his closeness to Jahangir King increased. In the last days of Jahan, he was assigned to the governorship of Agra and was in charge of all the treasures of the fort there. Your position was five thousand foot and five hundred cavalry. On the orders of Shah Jahan Badshah, he fought fiercely against the Portuguese of Bengal and used to grind their teeth. In this battle, ten thousand Portuguese were killed and about one thousand Muslims were also martyred, but Syed Qasim Baraha conquered the fort of Mangali. He died three days after starting this campaign. Jama Masjid of Agra city is the memorial of Nawab Syed Qasim Khan Bara. This mosque was built by him. An interesting incident related to Nawab Syed Qasim Khan Baraha, which is very famous, is written here. See: Once upon a time the king of Jahanger asked for water to drink. Water was brought in an earthen jar. The jar was very fragile. When the hand of the water-bringer shook, the jug fell and broke. Jahangir looked at his colleague Nawab Sayyed Qasim Khan Baraha and immediately said, &quot;I was very fragile and could not be calmed down&quot;. Syed Sabahuddin Abdul Rahman - M. O Nawab Qasim Khan Barah has completed the poem immediately by reciting the stanza of Fa Badiha in response. It is among the nobles of the first row. You got a very high position and distinguished status in the royal service. There is a great discussion of your courage and bravery in history. The book &quot;Maasir al-Amra&quot; is written by Syed Dalir Khan in Persian as follows: Syed Dalir Khan was in the era of Aurangzeb. You are specialized in Baroda criminal in Mudan, Gujarat. In the seventeenth year, the procession dried up in Shah Jahan and the crown prince and Nigzeb during the reign of King Shah Jahan. Saif Khan alias Safi Khan took courage and captured the city of Ahmedabad and thus paid the right of salt. 50 In the 49th year of procession, when the king was in Gujrat, then his position was increased by five hundred, which made him very happy, and then together with Khwaja Abul Hasan, he occupied Young Manir. In the fourth year of Jalus, King Aurangzeb, Azam Khan, who was at Saida, posted him here, and he himself retired to his old taluk, and died about six years later in the year A.H. Sayyid Hasan&#39;s son succeeded him and held the post of 1,500 castes for three years. His second son Syed Khalil held the post of five hundred foot soldiers. In the book &quot;According to Dr. Bar Nair&#39;s book &quot;According to Dr. Bar Nair&quot;, the world-famous writer Syed Muhammad Hussain Sahib described an incident related to Syed Debir Khan in detail. He saw a place on the backside from where the foot soldiers climbed and attacked the enemy&#39;s fronts. could do After informing the Raja and Nigzeb about this situation, he sent some of his soldiers to this hill and he himself took the rest of his army and went to the opposing fronts as their support and guard. Because by chance and from Nigzeb&#39;s artillery, the firing had stopped. Because of this, a little late some 1,000 horsemen from Darashkoh&#39;s army came out from their fronts to attack Raja Rajrup, and among the Muslim Amirs of Nigzeb, first Dir Khan and then Shaikh Mir sent their respective armies. Together with such a vigorous attack, they reached their fronts and a good fight took place in which Shaikh Mir jo ha thi penned which we transcribe below for the further interest of the readers. But Sawar was fighting his soldiers and was killed by a gunshot, but one of his compatriots is fully shown by this incident, how brave Syed Dalir Khan was and how bravely he fought on the battlefield:- Aurang The situation of the battle between Zeb and Dara Shikoh is written in the &quot;Alamgir Nama&quot; by Dara in such a way that the hills in Nawah Ajmer were well fortified by blocking their gorges and Dara Shikoh&#39;s artillery was also suitable. The Amirs of Nigzeb did not have the courage to attack until three days had passed Was it by chance that the Raja Raj Rup of Jammu, the Hastani soldier, the Gula Pahari Sayyid, who was sitting behind, cleverly held his dead body in such a way that not only the enemy, but also his own soldier, ended the battle? It was not known that he was killed and Syed Dalir Khan boldly entered the front lines of Dara Shikoh and killed his famous chief with his own arrow and was also wounded and in these attacks Shah Nawaz Khan and many others were killed. Named chieftains were also killed, while the foot soldiers of Raja Rajrup made their mark on the hill and Raja Jai Singh also went to the aid of all these chieftains with his army. Dara Shikoh had already lost a lot of courage due to the courage and boldness of Raj Roop, the black king of Dara Shikoh, and Dara Shikoh himself was in such a state that he exchanged his begums out of desperation.

54 53 (5) (4) Syed Nooruddin Ali Khan Syed Najamuddin Ali Khan Syed Sirajuddin Ali Khan Alana Syed Morus Sadat Mohalla Juma Morus Sadat Mohalla Gur also located in the town of Janath 7: Syed Nasir Ali Khan Willa Wold) located in the town of Jansath Al-Wald ) Syed Zafar Ali Khan Al-Awali) So you also got a lot of rise. After the fall of Farrukh Seir King, when Qutb-ul-Mulk Syed Hasan Ali Khan along with King Rafi-ud-Daula left the capital Delhi to suppress Raja Jai Singh, he handed over the management and charge of the place to Syed Najamuddin Ali Khan. During the procession in the second year of Muhammad Shah Badshah, when his elder brother Amir al-Amra Syed Hussain Ali Khan was killed with a dagger. And Qutb-ul-Mulk Syed Hasan Ali Khan was returning to Delhi when he heard the news of the murder of Amir al-Amrar and was very sad and disappointed and he immediately sent some sharp soldiers to Delhi and sent instructions to Syed Najamuddin Ali Khan that he should Keep the situation under control until reaching (Qutb-ul-Mulk) and continue to maintain your possession. At the same time, Syed Najmuddin Ali Khan started the recruitment of a new army. On the day of the battle you were in the forefront and you fought with great bravery and after fighting bravely you were seriously injured. (Quoted by Masher Al-Amrar in English) He was the son of Syed Abdullah Khan alias Syed Mian. You and your family lost an eye in this fight. Later you are very famous for the arresting characteristic i.e. masculinity and bravery. King Muhammad was captured and imprisoned. When you were imprisoned, during the time of Farkh Seer, when your elder brother, Amir al-Amrar Syed Sabin Ali, one of your daughters, who was barely nine years old, was taken to his house by his family for safety, but later When the king came to know, he invited your daughter to his palace. Some of the nobles of the royal harem wanted this Dakhta to be married to King Muhammad Shah. When Qutb-ul-Mulk Syed Hasan Ali Khan said this, Ghosh Ghazar Khan and Qutb-ul-Mulk Syed Hasan Ali Khan Jalil-ul-Qadr took the positions. Finally, if Muhammad Mughiruddin Jahandar Shah Ghalib became the permanent king, it was still in Lahore, and only two or three months had passed since his accession to the throne, when the news became known that Prince Farrukh Seir was intending to do so. As soon as this news was heard, Jahan Dar Shah came to Delhi from Lahore and immediately deposed Syed Hasan Ali Khan Bar Hai from the province of Allahabad and replaced him with Raji Muhammad Khan Warda Khan Khanan in the province of Allahabad. Abdul Ghaffar Gardizi Nabira Sadr Jahan was appointed to the position of Deputy Governor and left. Syed Abdul Ghaffar went to Jamiat for seven or eight thousand and did not go to Allahabad. On the other hand, Syed Hasan Ali Khan Baraha, being informed on this occasion, sent Syed Abul Hasan Khan Bijapuri along with his Bakhshi with three to four thousand foot soldiers to fight against Abdul Ghaffar. Stayed at a distance of two or three miles. After spending four or five days in letters and messages, Sayyid Abdul Ghaffar started to move forward relying on the large number of troops and the abundance of artillery. At the same time Syed Saifuddin Ali Khan and Syed Najmuddin Ali Khan and Syed Sirajuddin Ali Khan arrived with the help of their brother Syed Hasan Ali Khan along with Dewan Ratan Chand Bahmara. 60 59 again attacked with full force and surrounded Sadat from all sides and trapped Sadat in trouble. The Battle of Ghamsan took place. Syed Sirajuddin Ali Khan was killed in a fight with two eminent Sadats. After the death of Syed Sirajuddin Ali Khan, the enthusiasm of the rest of the Sadats increased. Sena became superior and began to attack the enemy more and more. The result was that Abdul Ghaffar Gardizi had to run away from the field with his army to save his life with a broken heart and Sadat was fighting for victory. Syed Sirajuddin Ali Khan&#39;s body was sent to his native town of Jansath and buried in his Murdati Bagh (Pakka Bagh). He had an island which has now collapsed. Only minor traces remain. (Author) Syed Alam Ali Khan And the battle of Syed Tahur Ali Khan, Syed Alam Ali Khan was the son of Syed Nooruddin Ali Khan and the nephew of Amir al-Amra Rasit Hussain Ali Khan and Qutb Mulk Syed Hasan Ali Khan He was appointed as ruler of the Deccan at the time when he was barely fifteen or seventeen years old Sir Syed brothers namely Qutbul Mulk Syed Hasan Ali Khan and Uma Al-Amra Syed Hussain Ali Khan were deposed and imprisoned due to their bad position and conspiracy to kill them, after that some changes in the system of the empire became inevitable. Nizam-ul-Mulk was appointed ruler of Malwa by the order of the Sayyid brothers. And during many campaigns, such as the unsuccessful rebellion of Prince Nico Caesar and the battle at Agra Fort, he openly disagreed with Sadat, but Nizam-ul-Mulk, considering the time and circumstances, never dared to take a direct fight with Sadat. On reaching Malwa, Nizam-ul-Mulk got the full opportunity to vent his anger against Sadat. A few days after reaching here, Alam raised a mutiny and in one bold attack crossed the Narida river and captured the Deccan as far as the fort of Amirgarh and Burhanpur. In this attack, Nizam-ul-Mulk did not face much resistance from Sadat. On this occasion, all the Sadats who were there could not get immediate help from North India, so they also accepted the forced obedience of Nizam-ul-Mulk. When the Sayyid brothers were informed of the successful rebellion of Nizam-ul-Mulk in Agra, they immediately sent a stern instruction to Sayyid Tahur Ali Khan Dadlawar Ali Ajo who was performing the duties of ruler of the Deccan in the absence of Sayyid Alam Ali Khan. He should prepare to welcome Nizam-ul-Mulk and try to kill him after arresting him. So Syed Tahur Ali Khan Mir Bakshi immediately sent a letter

Translated Text (Page 31):
62 61 sent to Nizam-ul-Mulk and warned him that it is not good for a great amir like Nizam-ul-Mulk to wander in the jungles and spread rebellion and rebellion while avoiding the royal rulers. Therefore, he should appear immediately and appear in the presence of the king along with Sayyid Sahib. Every effort will be made to forgive his mistake. As soon as he found this region, Nizam-ul-Mulk fully felt the smell of danger for himself. So, without caring about the outcome, he hastily organized his army and attacked Syed Shahur Ali Khan. Syed Sahib did not expect such an early fight from Nizam-ul-Mulk and he was not fully prepared for it. When he saw the army of Nizam-ul-Mulk growing, filled with the enthusiasm and emotions of bravery, without organizing his army, he himself rode on an elephant and went out to fight against Nizam-ul-Mulk. After a minor skirmish, he was killed by a gunshot and the other leading people who were with him met their end. On the other hand, when Sayyid Alam Ali Khan, having marched from Aurangabad, reached Talab Parnala, which is sixteen kos from Burbanpur, and camped, he heard the news of the death of Mir Nabakhshi Syed Tahur Ali Khan. On hearing this news, he became uncontrollable with anger and got busy raising a fresh army to fight Nizam-ul-Mulk. Within a short period of time, he assembled a strong army, which included many brave men like Jawahar Khan, Muhammad Beg, Mane Khan along with his brother Walatullah and Syed Wali Muhammad Baraha. Apart from them, Ghalib Khan Dikni, Mirza Ali Bahadur, Muhammad Ashraf Khan, Tayyab Khan and Khwaja Rehmat Khan were also included in this Topapkhana and Shamsher Khan. After all the preparations were completed, he wanted to attack Nizam-ul-Mulk, but in the meantime he received a message from his son Qutb-ul-Mulk Sayyid Hasan Ali Khan from Agra, instructing him that Alam Ali Khan, why That he is not young and inexperienced for this campaign, so avoid war and try to make peace. If this is not possible, collect all your wealth and weapons and come to North India and together with your old friends, establish the system. Confront the nation. The message went on to say that if even this was distasteful to the dear nephew, he should avoid Nizam-ul-Mulk for the time being and return to Aurangabad and wait there for his uncles when they advanced, to accompany them with their bravery. Show the essence of Because Syed Alam Ali Khan was young, the enthusiasm of youth blinded him. He did not follow the advice of his uncle Qutb-ul-Mulk and prepared himself for war. As Nizam-ul-Mulk was very smart, he postponed the battle due to the rainy season and spent a few months like that. When the rains ended, the two armies faced each other. Nizam-ul-Mulk was a man of old age and experience, and the whole of the Deccan was covered by him, so he purposely pushed himself eight to ten miles a day and encouraged Sayyid Alam Khan to advance.

64 63 The result was that one day there came a point where in front of his army there were deep swamps whose upper surface was completely dry. There was a small hill in front of the swamp. Nizam-ul-Mulk&#39;s army quickly left the swamp and climbed the hill in front and encamped there, and with great haste, installed the To Nai etc., and fortified themselves there. Syed Alam was very happy to see that she just wanted the enemy to be defeated. They did not know that there is water in the lower level of hearts. Sayyid Alam attacked Nizam-ul-Mulk with great enthusiasm with about two thousand of his best cavalry. Syed Alam&#39;s army had to enter the swamp so that their horses would be submerged in water up to their waists and necks. Later, Nizam Mulk Fateh Jang sent Syed Alam Ali Khan&#39;s casket to the Amir al-Amra Syed Hussain Ali Khan. Amir al-Amra sent his coffin to his native town of Jansath, where he was buried on the plinth of Syed Saifuddin Ali Khal tomb. The burial place of Syed Tamhur Ali Khan Rola Durasti is located in the town of Miranpur (Muzaffarnagar district). 5 went and most of the riders died on the spot. Syed Alam Ali Khan&#39;s horse Qutb-ul-Mulk Syed Hasan Ali Khan addressed to Abdullah Khan, who was a very original and thoroughbred animal, took Syed Alam to the bank with great difficulty. On the other hand, the soldiers of Nizam-ul-Mulk reached the other bank and were eagerly waiting for Sayyid. As soon as Sayyid Alam Ali Khan reached the bank and advanced towards the hill, the foot soldiers of Nizam Mulk immediately riddled the body of Sayyid with gun bullets and he came down from the horse. The incident of Syed Alam Ali Khan&#39;s martyrdom is a living example of his immense bravery and courage. Even though this step of his taking the money from Nizam-ul-Mulk was taken in haste and was completely inappropriate, but still the mark of bravery and dedication he left in history is Rufadar Zafar Jang and Zirzam Muhammad. Farrukh Sir Badshah Amir Al-Amra Seyed Hussain Ali Khan Feroze War General Ahlam Muhammad Farrukh Sir Badshada (Kingshah Gir Brothers) His name was Hasan Ali. Baradar Khurd means Syed Hussain Ali Khan was extremely brave, outspoken and purposeful. 73 were born. It became the king&#39;s habit to ridicule the Sayyid brothers and deliberately obstruct their work. The situation worsened to such an extent that the Sayyid brothers, being fed up, gave up attending the court and took refuge in a corner. Farrukh Seer&#39;s mother, who used to treat the Syed brothers with great compassion, came to Qutb-ul-Mulk Syed Hasan Ali Khan and explained to him and asked him to forget all the previous things. He also assured that the king will not break any promises in the future. The two brothers will not face any obstacle in carrying out the affairs of the kingdom. After all these things were settled, both the brothers agreed to perform observation services again and started attending the court. For some time, relations were good and peace prevailed. But after some time a few Sardars resumed their work, as a result of which the relations between the King and the Sayyid brothers again deteriorated. The king made it illegal for both of them step by step and insulted them personally and their position. Under the undue pressure of other chiefs, the Thani king of Karna appointed Asayid Hussain Ali Khan as the governor of the Deccan. Later U Badal left for the Deccan unwillingly. Qutb-ul-Mulk Syed Hasan Ali Khan used to put aside all the work related to the prime ministership so that the affairs of the kingdom would not clash with the king again and again. He entrusted all matters related to his position to Raja Ratan Chand. The hometown of Tan Chand was also the town of Jansath. He was initially a follower of Sayyid Hussain Ali Khan, like Ratan Chand continued to carry out the tasks of the 3rd Sultanate. On the other hand, Ibadan Khan had come very close to the Shamiri king and was always filling the king&#39;s ears against the Sayyids. Shamir Ki of Ibadan Khan prepared a conspiracy with the participation of the king, according to which the two Sayyid brothers had to be destroyed. Coincidentally, Qutb-ul-Mulk Syed Hasan Ali Khan was exposed to the conspiracy to kill himself and he defended himself. But after this conspiracy, Qutb-ul-Mulk became very alert and cautiously informed his brother Khurd Amir al-Amrar Sayyid Hussain Ali Khan who was in the Deccan that the situation here was unfavorable and his honor and life were in danger. So please come to Delhi as soon as possible. As soon as this information was received, Amir Al-Umra Syed Hussain Ali Khan left for Delhi with a large army and after a few days&#39; journey, he stayed in the suburbs of Delhi. Without extending our narration further, here we narrate an incident related to Maharaja Ajit Ghe to expose King Farrukh Sir&#39;s scheming mind and his vindictiveness, which is the all-time satisfaction of the king and against the big chiefs. His bad habit of laying a hideous trap is completely exposed.

76 75 Maharaja Ajit Singh was initially a fierce opponent of the Mughals. The king was very tired of his disobedience. It was only the fate of the two Syed brothers who used their intelligence and politics to tame the cross. For the sake of King Farrukh Seer, the Sayyid brothers took the risk of fighting with Maharaja Ajit Singh. It was not surprising that there would have been a fierce fight between the two, but the timely threatening intervention of Amir al-Amrar Syed Hussain Ali Khan forced Maharaja Ajit Singh to make peace with the king and he accepted to attend the court. This was a great favor of the Syed brothers to King Mohammad Farrukh Sir. Every king seemed to be satisfied with the presence of Ajit Singh, but in fact he was still not satisfied. Some will try to do harm. This groundless suspicion made Farrukh Sir anxious and he hatched a new conspiracy against Jeet Singh and attempted to assassinate the Maharaja. But due to the outbreak of this conspiracy, this trick of the king could not be successful. The following incident which we have quoted from the famous book &quot;Tarikh Ta Dra Jatan&quot; is presented for the perusal of the readers to make two guesses. That King Farukh Sir Baza Har Hara used to meet with me and the Sardar with such regularity, but what a black heart and conspiratorial incident had happened inside him. See the incident: When Ajit Singh arrived in Delhi in connection with the holding of the royal court, the king sent Bara Bhimkotawala and Khan Duran Khan to the Holy See. Ajit Singh was present at the bar. The King held Ajit Singh in high esteem. In addition to the position of seven thousand and increased crores, the rank of fisher. Elephants and horses. Swords and daggers on a minimalistic head. Garnished with pearls and khilaat. When Ajit Singh departed from here, Qutb-ul-Mulk Abdullah Khan escorted him with great pomp and ceremony. Both decided that the agreement was mutual. The Mughals (Kings) were afraid and the bushes would hide in such places and wait to somehow cut off Ajit Singh&#39;s life. We have also written this incident here. Now we continue our previous statement. Hussain Ali Khan was more arrogant than his elder brother Qutb-ul-Mulk Syed Hasan Ali Khan. Elderly Amrar Hussain Ali Khan used to make eye contact. When you were in a state of anger, you became even more terrifying. A map of the situation at the time when he came and settled in Delhi at the request of his elder brother has been beautifully presented by Alex Mender-Tod in &quot;History of Rajasthan&quot;. Jastan Tulfa: Alexander Tau

Translated Text (Page 39):
78 77 At Phagan, Ajit Singh and Syed appeared to kiss the king&#39;s feet. Both agreed to summon Hussain Ali Khan from the Deccan. In those days, the color of time was different. Bad omens were happening both in the sky and on earth, towards which a meteorite volcano was to be seen in front of the eyes. Siyar cried incessantly. The dogs were barking. There was no cloud, but the crackling of lightning and the thunder of the clouds used to tear the curtains of the ears. The splendor of the court was completely gone and the person was convinced that some calamity was going to happen in Dahi. Hussain Ali Khan came to Delhi later in the day. His face was terrifying. The sound of the bullies of the fort seemed sad. Although only a thousand riders were with him, it was known that Delhi was hidden by the dust. He stayed in the north of the city and kept in touch with Ajit Singh and his brother Abdullah Khan. The Mughal nobles were terrified as if out of fear. After reaching the end of Farrukh Seer&#39;s Sultanate, Amir Al-Amra Sayyid Hussain Ali Khan sent a personal message to the king in which he was asked to either hand over the management of the fort to him or else. Otherwise, he would not obey the orders of the king. This message made Pakar Badshah a little confused, but still handed over all the services and arrangements related to the fort to the Amir al-Amra. Amir al-Amra appointed his special men at all places of the fort and made the security measures more stringent. After that, the nobles entered the fort in the presence of the king and after a short meeting returned to their tent outside Dahi. On the second day, on the second day of February, Amir Al-Amra entered Delhi with a large number of soldiers for the purpose of meeting the king and stayed at Shaista Khan&#39;s mansion. A large number of soldiers were also kept there. Later, Qutb Mulk and Maharaja Ajit Singh entered the fort and took the keys of the fort in their possession for the purpose of proper administration. They spent all day and all night in the fort. Till that time, the people of Delhi were completely unaware of all the changes in the fort. Early in the morning, the news spread in the city that Qutb-ul-Mulk had been killed and that the royal forces were moving towards Delhi from the flanks to confront the Amir al-Amra. Amir al-Amra was greatly disturbed on hearing this news and immediately sent a message to Qutb-ul-Mulk that the situation was now out of control and it was necessary for his own safety to remove the king from the path. which has become the child of heinous conspiracies, so Qutb-ul-Mulk arrested King Farrukh Seir on February 18 and put him in prison and Rafi-ul-Darraj bin Rafi-ul-Shan bin Shah Alam was released from prison and placed him on the throne of Delhi. 80 79 &quot;History of Farrukh Seir&#39;s capture in Rajasthan is recorded as follows: The second day Salah was heard in Ajit Singh&#39;s tent on the banks of the Yamuna. Ajit Singh put his foot in the stirrup. Rathor accompanied him in the fort, the same condition as the king. When the sun came out, the king was captured The chaos that had played out among the people of Delhi ended with the accession of two Rafi-ul-Derajs. The prince was sick during his imprisonment, and he took care of his health even more, as a result of which he only died. He passed away after three months and a few days of completing the tasks of the kingdom. According to the will of Rafi-ud-Daraj, his elder brother Rafi-ud-Daula ascended the throne under the care of Amir al-Amrar and Qutb-ul-Mulk and was named Shah Jahan II. In the meantime, Prince Niko Sesar wanted to raise a rebellion in Agra and raised a commotion. To crush this rebellion, Amir Al-Amrar Syed Hussain Ali Khan took the king Rafi-ud-Daula with him to Agra. He left for Alexander-Tad and on reaching there he crushed the rebellion with strictness and established peace and order. In this way, when this rebellion failed and the fort was taken away, the golden dream of Niko Sir was shattered. Some time later, Jai Singh Sawai fought against the king at Fatehpur Sikri. So Qutb-ul-Mulk Syed Hasan Ali Khan along with King Rafi-ud-Daula left for Jai Singh. But Qutb-ul-Mulk managed to subdue Jai Singh by his clever stratagem and instead of fighting he was able to negotiate a peace with him. After this incident, King Rafi-ud-Daula also died of cholera after ruling for three months. After the death of Rafa-ud-Daula, prince Roshan Akhtar bin Jahan Shah bin Shah Alam was summoned from the Agra Fort and installed on the throne of September Khana in Delhi and his title was given as Muhammad Shah. Fall of Sayyid brothers Amir al-Amrar Sayyid Hussain Ali Khan and Qutb-ul-Mulk Sayyid Hasan Ali Khan never recognized themselves as the king, nor did they try to make themselves the king by force. He always promoted one or the other prince from the Timurid family to the throne of the empire. But after the capture of Muhammad Farrukh Seir, the situation had taken a different direction and the Sayyid brothers could no longer breathe China. It was at that time that chaos spread everywhere in the Mughal Empire

ہوا تھا اور گڑا بڑ تیزی سے بڑھتی جارہی تھی۔ یہ شورشیں بعد میں سید بھائیوں

82 81 was windy and the mess was increasing rapidly. These revolts later proved to be the forerunner of the downfall of the Syed brothers. At the beginning of May, the news was received that Nawab Nizam-ul-Mulk crossed the Narbada river from Malwa and captured Mirgarh fort and the city of Burhanpur. dispatched But Syed Dilawar Ali was killed by a gunshot after a brief skirmish. Later, Syed Alam Ali Khan, the deputy governor of the Deccan, fought against Nawab Nizam-ul-Mulk, but he too could not succeed in this campaign and he also sacrificed his life with great bravery. After hearing the news of the sad death of Alam Ali Khan, Amir al-Umra Rushit Hussain Ali Khan himself, along with the king, left for the Deccan for the purpose of correcting the mood of Nizam al-Mulk. They came to Pur up to four kos and then on September 11, they left for Delhi, taking many nobles with them. The dagger was stuck in his side, and due to severe pain, he came to the ground and after cursing the murderer, hit him on the face in such a way that he fell face down on the ground. Meanwhile, a group of Sadat&#39;s soldiers reached there and the murderer was killed on the spot. But Amir al-Iram could not die from the injury of Dagha. Hearing the ominous news of the killing of Amir al-Amra, his brother and Qutb-ul-Mulk Syed Hasan Ali Khan felt a great shock and he felt that all his forces were immediately united. Now Muntazar dar Syed Najamuddin Ali Khan, who was the administrator of Delhi Khas, was instructed by a swift messenger to immediately remove any prince from the prison and put him on the throne of the kingdom. So Syed Najamuddin Ali Khan enthroned Prince Sultan Ibrahim Bin Rafi Al Shan on October 7th. After a gap of two days, Qutb-ul-Mulk also reached Delhi. On reaching here, he took further measures to improve the existing army and along with this some new army was also recruited and Qutb-ul-Mulk was just on his way to Delhi when on 29th September he started supplying war supplies. That as soon as possible a better and stronger soldier should be suddenly transferred to him by his brother Amir al-Amra Syed Hussain Ali Khan. During his prime ministership, it was reported that Qutb-ul-Mulk collected as much cash as possible - the Amir-e-Amra was killed by Shaari by Mir Haider. What was God only knows how much, they all approached you under the pretense of presenting that accursed petition of this new army and spending it on their friends and permission. Qutb-ul-Mulk said that he submitted the petition after being summoned. As soon as I read the petition, if I live, I can get it back in cash, but if God&#39;s will is different, why should I leave it for others? While I was busy, this tyrant seriously stabbed Abdar with a dagger.

دونوں کو ماننا پڑے گا کہ دونوں بھائی اخلاق مجسم تھے ۔ بہادری میں کلام

ان دونوں بھائیوں کے ہاتھ ضرور رنگے پاؤگے لیکن یہ ملک داری اور حکومت
کے کرشمے تھے ان میں پڑ کر کوئی سلامت نہیں نکلا کرتا ہے "
قطب الملک اور امیر الامرار دونوں بھائیوں کے خاتمہ کے بعد سادات بار
کے اقبال کا ستارہ پوری طرح گردش میں آگیا تھا اور یہ قوم بڑی سبکی

In 88 87 there was a severe famine and accidentally a fire broke out in Pahar Ganje, which burnt down large stores of grain and houses etc. In addition, the lack of water for fallowing grain caused more rain which was always present in this area. At that time, Qutb-ul-Mulk Syed Hasan Ali Khan Rozeer-e-Azam, realizing the great suffering of the people of God, suggested the drainage of this canal using his generosity and wisdom. Which is mentioned above. Along with the removal of the canal, the repair of Bani Karim or Qadam Sharif was also carried out with some modifications and Qutb-ul-Mulk cut this blessed stone into two pieces and installed one footprint in the Delhi building and the other footprint in his own house. Jansath was sent to the native town. Syed Nooruddin Ali Khan, the brother of Haqiqi Qutb-ul-Mulk, was building his palace at that time in Mohalla Juma, town of Jansath, and he installed this stone at the place where it is now installed and is still known as the Prophet. This place is still a place of pilgrimage in the town. Chaudhry Bani Ahmed Sandelvi&#39;s statement about the qualities and excellent character of both Sayyid brothers, which is in his book Waqa&#39;i Alam Gir, is quoted here, which shows the excellence of character and high morals of both Sayyid brothers. Explained. See: Creativity, courage, Haidari and generosity are the legacy of Hashemi Sadat Azam. Outside the complex and thorny streets of governance, if these two brothers are weighed, they will come down in these qualities. Both friends and enemies will have to admit that both brothers were the embodiment of morality. Bravery has no words and generosity has proverbs. Khan Nusrat is the blood of war, the hands of these two brothers will surely be dyed, but it was the charisma of the country and the government, there is no peace in them. The star had come into full circulation and this nation began to decline with great ease When Sadat was twelve, he became a victim of these narrow-minded and narrow-minded nobles, and thus a large number of Sadats were executed After the death of his elder brothers, he returned to his native town, but after some time, the amirs of Muhammad Shah took him started troubling him and forced him to face the Muhammad Shahi forces which resulted in his defeat and an honorable death.

Translated Text (Page 45):
90 89 Syed Saifuddin Ali Khan Ibn Syed Abdullah Khan Baraha was the third son of Abdullah Khan alias Syed Mian. At the end of Aurangzeb&#39;s era, he entered the reign of the Universal King. After the death of Alamgir, when there was a dispute among his sons about the succession to the throne, he along with his brothers participated in the army of Moazzam Shah and showed bravery and courage on the occasion and after the accession of Moazzam Shah, he held the position of Jalila. happened After the death of Muhammad Azam Shah, when his elder son Miruddin Jahandar Shah deposed his elder brother Qutb-ul-Mulk Syed Hasan Ali Khan from the governorship of Allahabad and appointed Syed Abdul Faqar Gurdizi to take away the Allahabad Fort from him. Syed Hasan Ali Khan lined up against him, at that time Syed Saifuddin Ali Khan along with his other brothers would have reached the aid of his brother and when Muhammad Farrukh Sir and Jahan Dar Shah lined up, Syed Saif Ad-Din Ali Amir al-Amrara and Qutb-ul-Mulk were engaged in a battle by Muhammad Farrukh Sir with great activity. After this campaign was conducted and when Jahan Dar Shah was arrested, Farrukh Sir became the head of the kingdom, so he awarded him with the reward of modesty and khilaat, and awarded him the position of Hazari caste and two thousand cavalry. In Lillah Hijri, when Amir Al-Amra Syed Hussain Ali Khan received the news that Khand Panhar, like a general, was raising a rebellion in the regions and was trampling the whole country, and Zulfikar Bakshi, who was sent to his guard, When he was killed, Amir al-Amra appointed Syed Saifuddin Ali Khan to suppress him and appointed Raja Mohak Singh to help him. When Syed Saifuddin Ali Khan arrived in his territory, he was afraid of his arrival and ran away somewhere. Syed Sahib pursued him and reached the fort of Satara where he had taken refuge but still to no avail and he returned to Burhanpur. In 1 Hijri, Syed Saifuddin Ali Khan was with Amir Al-Amra and in Nigabad. A disagreement arose between Qutb-ul-Mulk and King Farrukh Sir, and Qutb-ul-Mulk summoned the Amir al-Amra to Delhi, so the Amir al-Amra sent Sayyid Saifuddin Ali Khan a few thousand horsemen to make the necessary arrangements and travel arrangements for Dubai. Ordered to march towards Pur. He immediately reached Burhanpur and before leaving for Delhi, he prepared all the necessary travel equipment, tools and artillery etc. In 2 Hijri, the reign of Roshan Akhtar Muhammad Shah Badshah came to the Sultanate and the Amir Al-Amir Syed Hussain Ali Khan was killed with a Dagger. After hearing the news of the murder of the Amirs, they were in agony. He at once intended to march towards Delhi and hastily assembled all the troops and supplies of war that could be procured.

94 93 was assigned to the criminal Saharanpur and sent him to his mind that you are being appointed so that all the Jagir of Syed Saifuddin Ali Khan should be confiscated and there would be no time to spoil it. hold up After coming to Saharanpur, Hashmat Khan started encroachment on his area Jagir. When he saw this, he humbly requested that Hazrat please forgive him for living in this area Jagir. But Heshmat Khan did not stop from his intention and hardened his attitude. When you saw that the honor and reputation of the family was in danger, you attacked Heshmat Khan and killed him. When Etimad-ud-Daulah Qamaruddin Khan got the news of the death of Heshmat Khan, blood came to his eyes and Syed Saifuddin Ali Khan got hold of the excuse of killing the army. He immediately appointed Azimullah Khan with Shakar Jarar to kill and loot Ranian Sadat and assigned Ali Muhammad Khan Rohila, Fariduddin Khan Azimullah Khan Farooqi and Shaikhzada Hai Lucknow Faujdar Moradabad to help him. When this Shukar encamped near Mauza Bhinsi, seven or eight miles from the town of Jansath, and this news reached Sayyid Saifuddin Ali Khan, he immediately sent his brothers, servants, loved ones and servants to R Josh Shujaat along with other Sadats. Ready to fight and went there. First, he inquired about the reason for coming to this side from Army Chief Halimullah Khan through Aichi, when it came to know that a raid had been made for the management of the deceased criminal, he apologized to him by expressing helplessness and coercion. of But Azimullah Khan did not listen to one and assembled his army and came forward. Even then, in spite of the small number of people and the absence of war equipment, cannons and rifles, you pushed forward with the courage of a man and fought so bravely that the enemies missed six shots. Suddenly, Nawab Ali Muhammad Khan Rohilla arrived with his fresh army for reinforcements. The confused feet of the Turanis froze again and they all surrounded Sadat from all sides and started firing with arrows and guns. Among all the men who were fighting on Sadat&#39;s side. Not one survived and all died very young. Syed Saifuddin Ali Khan also came in handy in this battle. Even with the murder of Syed Saifuddin Ali Khan, the queens did not come to China and they attacked the town of Jansath, which was the residence of the late Syed Sahib and his ancestors. Fearlessly returned to Sadat. After several days of desolation, Azimullah Khan escorted Syed Saifuddin Ali Khan to Delhi and presented him to King Muhammad Shah to please him. Later, Syed Saifuddin Ali Khan&#39;s body was brought to the town of Jansath and he was buried here. His magnificent tomb is still in excellent condition in the town. Maulvi Hakeem Muhammad Najm-ul-Ghani Rashid Saif-ud-Din Ali Khan&#39;s brief account of the competition with Muhammad Shahi&#39;s forces written in his book &quot;Akhbar Al-Sanadid Volume I&quot;

106 105 Syed Abdullah Khan Dakhandan Moti Mahal) Syed Sun Ali Khan Syed Mumtaz Ali Khan Syed Hasan Ali Khan Syed Ejaz Ali Khan Daughter of Syed Mohsin Ali Khan Daughter of Syed Mumtaz Ali Khan Syed Mushtaq Ali Khan Daughter of Syed Mushtaq Ali Khan 7 7 Chanda Tum Sadat The Secrets of Baraha&#39;s Donations After the fall of the Mughal Empire in India, when the British began to grow in power and the East India Company conquered the area between the Ganges and the Yamuna rivers in the beginning, Sadat Baraha&#39;s authority And dignitaries also carefully reviewed the situation and recognized the direction of the wind. So Sadat acted very wisely and offered his services to the British authorities and by his sincere services to them, he made the Ferangis completely loyal to him. In this way, there was no significant decrease in the honor and fame of Sadat Baraha even during the British rule. And because of their services, this nation continued to be equally blessed with the blessings of the British rulers and maintained its prominent position and glory. After the end of the English era and the subsequent partition of India, certain figures of Sadat Bahirah gained extraordinary fame. Syed Mehdi Ali Khan Syed Ahmad Ali Khan Syed Jad Ali Khan Dokhtar Dokhtar So we write a brief description of the selected personalities here so that the readers&#39; information about Sadat can be increased. کے حالات میں تبدیلی ناگزیر ہو گئی۔ ان تبدیوں کا انٹر یہ ہوا کہ جنگ و جدل

نہ دیا اور اخراجات ہمارے ہمیشہ سے ہی شاہانہ رہے علاوہ اس کے ابتدا سے

کو ہمیشہ بری نگاہ سے دیکھا اور ان کی تعلیم کو اہمیت نہ دی جس کی وجہ

Translated Text (Page 56):
112 111 Conclusion and Recommendation From the beginning, the tribe of Sadat Bara has been a warrior and due to its warrior qualities, it has gained immense popularity. Brave and courageous people were born in this nation, who defeated their contemporaries in the battlefield and established their legacy, whose history is still a witness today. It was Sadat&#39;s immense bravery that kept him in the forefront of the Mughal armies, which was clearly evidenced by his presence in every leading army. Along with this, Sadat risked his life in big battles and saved the Mughal orders. After the fall of the Mughal Empire in India, when the British came to power and established their dominance over the whole of India, a change in the conditions here became inevitable. The result of these changes was that the opportunities for war and controversy that were available to the nation have now completely disappeared. Therefore, in this way, the entire nation became physically weak. At the end of the English era, the general economic conditions of Sadat Bara started to deteriorate, while their jagirs etc. were confiscated, but even in these conditions, the general condition of Qawyim was satisfactory, although there was no abundance of luxury. After some time the situation took a new turn when the Zamindari system was abolished. Going to land ownership had an extremely unpleasant effect on the economic condition of the Sadats because most of the Sadats were content with land ownership and cultivation and this had become the profession of this nation. After the independence of the country, when Sadat&#39;s landholdings were no longer there, the nation made small farming as a means of livelihood and did not consider adopting any modern profession, which resulted in our economic conditions deteriorating and The whole nation was in an economic crisis. The reason for our poor economy was that we never paid attention to the development of our sources of income and our expenses were always lavish. We did not give priority to modern education and were always ignorant of knowledge. Although some families could afford the expenses of higher education, but they also did not pay any attention to it and did not care to equip their children with separate education. When the men of the nation were in this state, they only mentioned Mastorat. Our nation has always viewed women&#39;s education with a bad eye and did not give importance to their education due to which our women are deprived of knowledge. Due to all these reasons, the economic conditions of Sadat Barah became disorganized and gradually poverty engulfed the nation and pushed it towards the dark cave of misery and anonymity. The result was that physically we were already exhausted and now economically too

114 113 have become extremely weak. Along with the disruption of the economic system and the increase in illiteracy, other social and moral evils also arose in us, due to which our social structure was multiplied and the individuality of the nation was almost lost. Apart from this, due to the deterioration of the society, the national unity was greatly hurt and the Shiraza of the nation remained dispersed. Instead of mutual reconciliation and brotherhood, it has become our way to criticize and ridicule each other. The result of the deterioration of morals and the promotion of social defects was that we lost our national dignity and with it our power also departed. Now the situation is that other nations have overtaken us and we are far behind in this race of development. In the last half of the year, a few evils have occurred in our society, one of them is the attraction towards education. Now we have made some progress in the field of education. The importance of higher education is well understood. In the past years, many young people of Sadat Bara have given up their native profession of farming and after getting basic education, they have taken jobs in various fields. A large number of young people of Sadat Baraha have now taken up the profession of lawyers after getting their education. In this regard, Syed Kausar Ali Khan, resident of Jansath, Syed Roni Ali Zaidi, resident of Mouza Jawara, Syed Nazar Muhammad, resident of Mouza Belara, Syed Iqbal Abbas, resident of Muzaffarnagar, Syed Mahmood Ali, resident of Mouza Bashmpur, Syed Shahid Raza, resident of Mouza Balipora, Syed Nazar Hasnain. The names of Mauza Chitora, Syed Shabia Mustafa resident of Mauza Joli, Syed Lakhtman Mauza Sandha Wali etc. are worth mentioning. Apart from this, a few gentlemen have also taken the job of the education department, in this regard, Dr. Syed Iqbal Hussain Mouza Chitora (currently Muslim University Aligarh. Syed Zaheer Haider Mouza Beera Sadat Rehal Muslim University Aligarh) and Syed Anwar Ali Zaidi Kasbah Jansath ( Halal (Somalia - Africa) names are worth mentioning. The trend of getting mechanical education among the youth of Sadat is also increasing. A large number of married boys have joined the technical service. In this regard, the names of Syed Muhammad Mehdi Kasbah Jansath (Engineer) (now Iraq) and Sayyed Saadat Nabi Zaidi resident of Mauza Bihari are worth mentioning. Apart from them, a few other gentlemen are also doing 10301 training course (engineering). The educational trend is still very low among women compared to men. However, the economy of Sadat has improved a lot in the past few years. The financial condition of many families is improving and we still see a lot of progress in their lives Hard work is done to improve their conditions because most of the people of Sadat are still poor. 116 115 are also moving forward which is an encouraging step and its happy results will be visible in the next ten years. Create change in yourself keeping in mind the environment and demands. The most important thing for us is education. It is the duty of all people to try to make their children and youth educated as much as possible. There is enough scope for us in the field of technical education. After doing such training courses, new job opportunities will be provided to our youth. Therefore, there is a need to acquire mechanical education as much as possible so that our progress can be accelerated. There is also a need to pay special attention to women&#39;s education. If our girls are educated, they will have a better chance of shaping their future and will be able to raise their children in a better way, which will have an impact on future generations. Apart from education, the problem of improving the economy is also very difficult. Along with the development of education, our economy should also improve. The only proper way to do this is that we should do the work in the field with great effort and honesty. Those who take up the profession of agriculture will have to work hard and develop their profession using modern methods. In this regard, the current government is also providing sufficient assistance. Apart from this, those who are in government or private jobs should also perform their services with great effort and honesty so that the development paths are not blocked for them. In the end, I request all the people of the nation to give up their old habits and try hard to improve their social condition. The time has come to give up outdated and illegal rituals and customs. It is very important to promote mutual brotherhood. Do not take such actions that create a gap in the unity and consensus of the nation. Do not be jealous and jealous of each other, but take steps keeping in mind the principle of mutual aid. It is the duty of our brothers who are developed and happy to help their lesser brothers as much as possible so that they can also get a chance to move forward. However, after considering all these measures, if we follow them, there is no reason why we cannot compete with other developed nations and happiness will not kiss our feet and surely this is the real secret of prosperity. Is . Why should the survival of luxury be lost in this house of mortality, change it to time, then why should the dream be expensive? O nation, the pain of poverty is its cry.
